---
about_this_resource_text: <h2 class="subhead">Description</h2> <p>Associative array
  mathematics. Relevant operations on an associative array. Semirings and matrices.
  See MIT Press book &quot;Mathematics of Big Data.&quot;</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong>
  Jeremy Kepner</p>

  <span m="246940">Probably</span> <span m="248210">100</span> <span m="248710">million</span>

  <span m="261690">other.</span></p><p><span m="263620">Big</span> <span m="263940">tables,</span>

  <span m="767700">that</span> <span m="767900">way</span> <span m="768060">as</span>
  <span m="768170">well.</span> <span m="768480">So</span> <span m="768660">we</span>
  <span m="768770">support</span> <span m="769170">them</span> <span m="769280">both.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="772290">the</span> <span m="772410">core</span> <span m="773350">composable</span>

  <span m="1000780">quickly.</span></p><p><span m="1001230">So</span> <span m="1001240">that''s</span>
  <span m="1001440">a</span> <span m="1001460">very</span> <span m="1001670">powerful,</span>
  <span m="1002690">powerful</span> <span m="1003030">concept.</span> <span m="1003540">And

  <span m="1005380">course,</span> <span m="1005690">this</span> <span m="1005870">whole</span>
  <span m="1006560">concept</span> <span m="1007100">looks</span> <span m="1007320">very</span>
  <span m="1007520">much</span> <span m="1007770">like</span> <span m="1007950">an</span>
  <span m="1008040">associative</span> <span m="1008560">array.</span> <span m="1008750">Mathematically,</span>
  <span m="1009400">we</span> <span m="1009530">can</span> <span m="1009660">treat</span>
  <span m="1009910">it</span> <span m="1010060">as</span> <span m="1010310">an</span>
  <span m="1010400">associative</span> <span m="1010930">array.</span></p><p><span
  m="1025400">All</span> <span m="1025520">right.</span> <span m="1025780">So</span>
  <span m="1025920">that''s</span> <span m="1026150">sort</span> <span m="1026310">of</span>
  <span m="1026400">the easy</span> <span m="1026800">part.</span> <span m="1027900">I</span>
  <span m="1027950">think</span> <span m="1028140">we''ve</span> <span m="1028310">covered</span>
  <span m="1028619">a</span> <span m="1028680">lot</span> <span m="1028890">of</span>
  <span m="1028950">this</span> <span m="1029109">before</span> <span m="1029490">in</span>
  <span m="1029619">previous</span> <span m="1030010">lectures.</span> <span m="1030450">Now,</span>
  <span m="1030609">we''re</span> <span m="1030730">going</span> <span m="1030819">to</span>
  <span m="1030869">get</span> <span m="1031010">into</span> <span m="1031260">some</span>
  <span m="1031460">of</span> <span m="1031520">the</span> <span m="1031579">more</span>
  <span m="1032430">mathematical</span> <span m="1033280">elements,</span> <span m="1034069">which</span>
  <span m="1034250">aren''t</span> <span m="1034430">necessarily</span> <span m="1035069">hard.</span>
  <span m="1036140">They</span> <span m="1036420">just</span> <span m="1037520">impose</span>

  <span m="1041960">don''t</span> <span m="1042220">necessarily</span> <span m="1042960">use</span>

  <span m="1043839">day</span> <span m="1044010">to</span> <span m="1044099">day</span>
  <span m="1044569">work</span> <span m="1044839">lives.</span> <span m="1045970">So</span>
  <span m="1046170">we''re</span> <span m="1046290">going</span> <span m="1046380">to</span>
  <span m="1046420">talk</span> <span m="1046660">about</span> <span m="1047190">what

  <span m="1051480">like</span> <span m="1051630">matrix</span> <span m="1051970">multiply.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="1059540">treat</span> <span m="1061130">an</span> <span m="1061260">associative</span>
  <span m="1061890">array</span> <span m="1062520">as</span> <span m="1062640">sets</span>
  <span m="1062980">of</span> <span m="1063110">keys</span> <span m="1063540">and</span>
  <span m="1063680">values</span> <span m="1065060">that</span> <span m="1065180">are</span>
  <span m="1065300">drawn</span> <span m="1066490">from</span> <span m="1066740">infinite</span>
  <span m="1067200">strict</span> <span m="1067520">totally</span> <span m="1067840">ordered</span>
  <span m="1068190">set,</span> <span m="1068700">we''ll</span> <span m="1068820">call</span>
  <span m="1069060">it</span> <span m="1069190">S.</span> <span m="1070250">You might</span>
  <span m="1070350">be like,</span> <span m="1070660">what</span> <span m="1070980">is</span>
  <span m="1071230">that?</span> <span m="1072150">What</span> <span m="1072330">is</span>
  <span m="1072460">an</span> <span m="1072610">infinite strict</span> <span m="1073340">totally</span>
  <span m="1073630">ordered</span> <span m="1073820">set?</span></p><p><span m="1074310">It''s</span>
  <span m="1074560">just</span> <span m="1074840">a</span> <span m="1074910">set</span>
  <span m="1075230">where</span> <span m="1075370">there''s</span> <span m="1075580">an</span>
  <span m="1075730">ordering,</span> <span m="1077140">where</span> <span m="1077250">basically</span>

  <span m="1080520">you</span> <span m="1082420">one</span> <span m="1082850">is</span>
  <span m="1083030">greater</span> <span m="1083320">than</span> <span m="1083480">the</span>
  <span m="1083640">other.</span> <span m="1084410">And</span> <span m="1084480">they</span>

  <span m="1086400">So</span> <span m="1086680">it</span> <span m="1086720">will</span>
  <span m="1086880">tell</span> <span m="1087070">you</span> <span m="1087270">that,</span>
  <span m="1087680">you know,</span> <span m="1088200">to give</span> <span m="1088310">it</span>
  <span m="1088520">any</span> <span m="1088740">two</span> <span m="1088870">values,</span>
  <span m="1089270">I</span> <span m="1089320">can</span> <span m="1089470">ask</span>
  <span m="1089660">the</span> <span m="1089750">question</span> <span m="1090160">is</span>
  <span m="1091060">one</span> <span m="1091280">greater</span> <span m="1091570">than</span>
  <span m="1091690">the</span> <span m="1091820">other</span> <span m="1092130">or</span>
  <span m="1092385">are</span> <span m="1092640">they</span> <span m="1092860">equal?</span>
  <span m="1093170">So</span> <span m="1093300">that''s</span> <span m="1093560">the</span>
  <span m="1093650">strict</span> <span m="1094050">part.</span></p><p><span m="1096310">So</span>
  <span m="1097040">that</span> <span m="1097360">encompasses</span> <span m="1098350">a</span>
  <span m="1098430">lot.</span> <span m="1100800">Obviously,</span> <span m="1101500">it</span>

  <span m="1105460">that.</span> <span m="1105620">But it</span> <span m="1105730">also</span>

  <span m="1119150">that.</span> <span m="1119370">We</span> <span m="1119470">always</span>
  <span m="1119710">use</span> <span m="1119860">lexicographic</span> <span m="1120480">ordering.</span>
  <span m="1120880">We</span> <span m="1120960">don''t</span> <span m="1121100">really</span>
  <span m="1121270">have</span> <span m="1121520">another</span> <span m="1122700">ordering</span>

  <span m="1123880">at</span> <span m="1124540">our</span> <span m="1124670">disposal.</span></p><p><span
  m="1127110">So</span> <span m="1127290">given</span> <span m="1127910">those</span>
  <span m="1128390">keys</span> <span m="1128990">and</span> <span m="1129210">values,</span>
  <span m="1131060">an</span> <span m="1131190">associative</span> <span m="1131930">array</span>
  <span m="1133770">is</span> <span m="1134000">a</span> <span m="1134090">partial</span>
  <span m="1134660">function</span> <span m="1136360">from</span> <span m="1136650">a</span>
  <span m="1138150">d</span> <span m="1138490">dimensional</span> <span m="1139040">set</span>
  <span m="1139350">of</span> <span m="1139500">keys</span> <span m="1141126">to</span>
  <span m="1142440">a</span> <span m="1142540">value.</span> <span m="1143520">So</span>
  <span m="1143790">if</span> <span m="1144060">we</span> <span m="1144170">have</span>
  <span m="1144430">the</span> <span m="1144510">vector</span> <span m="1145110">of</span>
  <span m="1145200">key,</span> <span m="1145620">so</span> <span m="1146390">typically</span>
  <span m="1146950">d</span> <span m="1147270">will</span> <span m="1147460">be</span>
  <span m="1147720">2.</span> <span m="1148940">And</span> <span m="1150200">the</span>
  <span m="1150330">first</span> <span m="1150700">k1</span> <span m="1151240">will</span>
  <span m="1151380">be</span> <span m="1151600">the</span> <span m="1151730">row</span>

  <span m="1153010">a</span> <span m="1153120">column</span> <span m="1153540">key.</span>
  <span m="1154340">And</span> <span m="1154490">it</span> <span m="1154540">will</span>
  <span m="1154660">map</span> <span m="1154950">out</span> <span m="1155060">its</span>
  <span m="1156260">partial</span> <span m="1156630">function</span> <span m="1159570">from</span>
  <span m="1159970">the d</span> <span m="1160100">keys</span> <span m="1160830">to</span>
  <span m="1161000">one</span> <span m="1161350">value.</span></p><p><span m="1162440">So</span>
  <span m="1162980">it</span> <span m="1163070">will</span> <span m="1163260">look</span>
  <span m="1163500">like</span> <span m="1163790">this,</span> <span m="1164740">an</span>
  <span m="1164830">associative</span> <span m="1165440">array</span> <span m="1168150">with</span>
  <span m="1169030">a</span> <span m="1169130">vector</span> <span m="1169435">of</span>
  <span m="1169740">keys,</span> <span m="1170540">typically</span> <span m="1171100">2.</span>
  <span m="1172300">I</span> <span m="1172920">will</span> <span m="1173080">have</span>
  <span m="1173520">a</span> <span m="1173590">value</span> <span m="1175930">vi</span>
  <span m="1177800">and</span> <span m="1178020">that it</span> <span m="1178200">is</span>
  <span m="1178610">empty</span> <span m="1179260">otherwise.</span> <span m="1182350">So</span>
  <span m="1182570">this</span> <span m="1182810">is</span> <span m="1183770">its</span>
  <span m="1183960">function,</span> <span m="1184310">because</span> <span m="1184530">we</span>
  <span m="1184710">only</span> <span m="1185030">define</span> <span m="1185430">it</span>
  <span m="1186280">where</span> <span m="1186520">these</span> <span m="1186800">keys</span>
  <span m="1187160">exist.</span></p><p><span m="1188310">So</span> <span m="1188470">you</span>
  <span m="1188630">can</span> <span m="1188970">Imagine</span> <span m="1189380">that</span>
  <span m="1189520">every</span> <span m="1189845">singe</span> <span m="1190170">associative</span>
  <span m="1190900">array</span> <span m="1192060">is</span> <span m="1192360">a</span>
  <span m="1192500">function</span> <span m="1193140">over</span> <span m="1193390">the</span>
  <span m="1193540">entire</span> <span m="1194250">space</span> <span m="1194700">of</span>
  <span m="1194810">all</span> <span m="1195070">possible</span> <span m="1195650">keys.</span>
  <span m="1196660">But</span> <span m="1196760">we''re</span> <span m="1196970">only</span>
  <span m="1197290">giving</span> <span m="1197590">you</span> <span m="1197700">the</span>
  <span m="1197820">ones</span> <span m="1198310">that</span> <span m="1198430">are</span>
  <span m="1198520">defined.</span> <span m="1199630">And</span> <span m="1199800">everywhere</span>
  <span m="1200340">else,</span> <span m="1200620">it''s</span> <span m="1200780">undefined.</span>
  <span m="1202070">OK.</span></p><p><span m="1202770">This</span> <span m="1203080">is</span>
  <span m="1203220">actually</span> <span m="1203560">a</span> <span m="1203620">fairly</span>
  <span m="1204180">large</span> <span m="1204580">break</span> <span m="1204920">from</span>
  <span m="1205110">linear</span> <span m="1205400">algebra,</span> <span m="1206460">where</span>
  <span m="1206610">we</span> <span m="1207270">can</span> <span m="1207430">have</span>
  <span m="1208840">functions--</span> <span m="1211610">a</span> <span m="1211930">matrix</span>
  <span m="1212350">is</span> <span m="1212450">really</span> <span m="1212640">a</span>
  <span m="1212690">function</span> <span m="1213090">of</span> <span m="1213160">the</span>
  <span m="1213300">indices,</span> <span m="1214010">the</span> <span m="1214260">ij</span>
  <span m="1214630">indices,</span> <span m="1215120">which</span> <span m="1215320">are</span>
  <span m="1215410">integers.</span> <span m="1216520">Here,</span> <span m="1216690">we</span>
  <span m="1216840">allow</span> <span m="1216990">them</span> <span m="1217100">to</span>
  <span m="1217160">be</span> <span m="1217320">anything.</span> <span m="1218430">And</span>
  <span m="1218620">we</span> <span m="1218770">formally</span> <span m="1219440">support</span>
  <span m="1219850">the</span> <span m="1219950">concept</span> <span m="1220680">of</span>
  <span m="1220800">a</span> <span m="1220880">completely</span> <span m="1222270">empty</span>
  <span m="1222710">row</span> <span m="1223010">or</span> <span m="1223120">column.</span></p><p><span
  m="1223890">So</span> <span m="1224020">associative</span> <span m="1224530">arrays</span>
  <span m="1224960">don''t</span> <span m="1225220">allow</span> <span m="1225630">that.</span>
  <span m="1227470">They</span> <span m="1227620">only</span> <span m="1228310">store</span>
  <span m="1229420">not</span> <span m="1229770">empty</span> <span m="1230160">information.</span>
  <span m="1231580">And</span> <span m="1231750">in</span> <span m="1231850">our</span>
  <span m="1232000">implementation,</span> <span m="1232820">we</span> <span m="1232960">tend</span>
  <span m="1233220">to</span> <span m="1233300">store</span> <span m="1233890">0</span>
  <span m="1235120">as</span> <span m="1237520">equivalent</span> <span m="1238070">to</span>
  <span m="1238320">null</span> <span m="1239330">in</span> <span m="1239500">this</span>
  <span m="1239680">space.</span> <span m="1240110">Because</span> <span m="1240490">the</span>
  <span m="1240610">underlying</span> <span m="1241230">sparse</span> <span m="1241640">matrix</span>
  <span m="1242110">implementation</span> <span m="1243230">does</span> <span m="1243530">that.</span></p><p><span
  m="1243820">0</span> <span m="1244320">is</span> <span m="1244440">essentially</span>
  <span m="1244950">treated</span> <span m="1245340">as</span> <span m="1245510">the</span>
  <span m="1245610">null</span> <span m="1245970">character.</span> <span m="1247180">So</span>
  <span m="1248200">that''s</span> <span m="1248400">a</span> <span m="1248440">big</span>
  <span m="1248730">difference.</span> <span m="1250290">Now,</span> <span m="1250480">we</span>
  <span m="1250610">can</span> <span m="1250750">still</span> <span m="1250980">use</span>
  <span m="1251400">our</span> <span m="1251520">linear</span> <span m="1251780">algebraic</span>
  <span m="1252240">intuition,</span> <span m="1253870">but</span> <span m="1254050">that''s</span>
  <span m="1254590">the</span> <span m="1254750">fundamental</span> <span m="1256150">difference</span>
  <span m="1256540">here.</span></p><p><span m="1258890">So</span> <span m="1259140">binary</span>
  <span m="1259820">operations</span> <span m="1260620">on</span> <span m="1260800">any</span>
  <span m="1261030">two</span> <span m="1261180">associative</span> <span m="1261700">arrays--</span>
  <span m="1262280">so</span> <span m="1262530">I have</span> <span m="1262680">associative</span>
  <span m="1263120">array</span> <span m="1263280">A1</span> <span m="1263650">and</span>
  <span m="1263760">A1</span> <span m="1264080">with</span> <span m="1264240">this</span>
  <span m="1264410">binary</span> <span m="1264800">operation--</span> <span m="1269050">are</span>
  <span m="1270030">defined</span> <span m="1271380">essentially</span> <span m="1271950">by</span>
  <span m="1272150">two</span> <span m="1272480">functions.</span> <span m="1274680">The</span>
  <span m="1274830">sort</span> <span m="1275020">of</span> <span m="1275180">upper</span>
  <span m="1275590">function</span> <span m="1276090">here</span> <span m="1276720">says</span>
  <span m="1277060">how</span> <span m="1277310">we''re</span> <span m="1277500">going</span>
  <span m="1277610">to</span> <span m="1277710">treat</span> <span m="1278120">the</span>
  <span m="1278260">keys.</span> <span m="1280260">So</span> <span m="1280370">if</span>
  <span m="1280450">we</span> <span m="1280620">have</span> <span m="1280830">two</span>
  <span m="1281230">associate</span> <span m="1281750">arrays,</span> <span m="1283020">their</span>
  <span m="1283280">keys,</span> <span m="1284250">some</span> <span m="1284510">of</span>
  <span m="1284550">them</span> <span m="1284710">can</span> <span m="1284860">overlap.</span>
  <span m="1285820">Some</span> <span m="1286060">of</span> <span m="1286110">them</span>
  <span m="1286270">cannot</span> <span m="1286750">overlap.</span> <span m="1287640">And</span>
  <span m="1287780">our</span> <span m="1287870">function</span> <span m="1288490">will</span>
  <span m="1288680">either</span> <span m="1288910">choose</span> <span m="1289370">to</span>
  <span m="1290110">look</span> <span m="1290300">for</span> <span m="1290450">the</span>
  <span m="1290770">union</span> <span m="1291320">or</span> <span m="1291480">the</span>
  <span m="1291680">intersection</span> <span m="1292440">of</span> <span m="1292620">those.</span></p><p><span
  m="1293920">So</span> <span m="1294650">for</span> <span m="1294760">instance,</span>
  <span m="1295160">if</span> <span m="1295170">we</span> <span m="1295290">do</span>
  <span m="1295490">addition,</span> <span m="1296560">that''s</span> <span m="1296910">most</span>
  <span m="1297440">associated</span> <span m="1298150">with</span> <span m="1298280">unioning</span>
  <span m="1300970">the</span> <span m="1301130">underlying</span> <span m="1301710">keys.</span>
  <span m="1303700">If</span> <span m="1304000">we</span> <span m="1304260">do</span>
  <span m="1305750">other</span> <span m="1306030">operations,</span> <span m="1306960">like</span>
  <span m="1307360">and,</span> <span m="1308610">that''s</span> <span m="1309040">most</span>
  <span m="1309300">consistent</span> <span m="1310040">with</span> <span m="1311090">intersecting</span>
